Program support is provided on musescore.org.\r\n\r\n\r\nFeatures supported by MuseScore include:\r\n\r\n* Unlimited score length\r\n* Unlimited number of staves per system\r\n* Up to four independent voices per staff\r\n* Score creation wizard and templates\r\n* Guitar, bass, ukulele, lute tablature\r\n* Automatic part extraction and transposition\r\n* Repeats, including segnos, codas, and measure repeats\r\n* Dynamics, articulations, and other expression markings, with playback support for most\r\n* Custom text markings\r\n* Lyrics\r\n* Chord symbols\r\n* Jazz notation, including lead sheets, slash notation and a “handwritten” font for text\r\n* Swing and shuffle playback\r\n* Mixer for instrument levels and effects\r\n* Percussion notation\r\n* Early music notation\r\n* Cross-staff beaming\r\n* Import of graphics\r\n* Custom key signatures\r\n* Additive time signatures\r\n* User-defined score styles\r\n\r\nMost elements in MuseScore are laid out automatically but can also be positioned manually. The capabilities of MuseScore can be extended via plugins, and the growing repository on musescore.org contains many plugins submitted by users.\r\n\r\nMuseScore includes a set of sounds that reproduce common instruments (as defined by General MIDI) without taking up a lot of disk space or memory, but you can also substitute any SoundFont you prefer for a wider variety of sounds or for more realism.\r\n\r\nMuseScore can import and export MIDI and MusicXML files, and it can also import from Capella and several other programs. For example: “Read 30 pages tomorrow at 8PM #books” will set a task for tomorrow, at 8PM in your Books project. \r\nComplete your tasks directly from the notification toast and easily pick up where you left off with Windows Timeline. \r\nRemember deadlines and build lasting habits with recurring due dates like \"every second Monday\".\r\nFree up mental space by assigning tasks to people in your shared projects.\r\nHighlight your day’s most important activities with color-coded priority levels.\r\nSee your daily and weekly progress with beautifully customized productivity graphs.\r\nMake the most of your Windows 10 device with unique, Windows-specific features like support for Live Tiles, jump list, and a beautifully designed 3rd panel view. \r\n\r\nYou can convert Todoist into your central, organized hub for getting things done with access to 60+ popular app integrations like Dropbox, Amazon Alexa, Zapier, IFTTT, and Slack. \r\n\r\nTodoist is free forever with the option to upgrade to Todoist Premium. With Todoist Premium, you’ll enjoy unlimited access to powerful features that’ll help you achieve your goals faster while feeling confident and in control. \r\n\r\nTeams and small business collaborate more efficiently with the Business plan.
